FK `ON DELETE SET NULL`; the payer is a Bill-To entity, **not** a customer — MRR/acceptance/reporting stay keyed on the homeowner, AR rolls to the payer.

**Resolution + safety (`server/services/payer.js`):** `resolveForInvoice()` and `attachToInvoice()` **never throw** — a payer lookup can never block invoicing; both fail soft to self-pay. A **deactivated** payer link also falls back to self-pay rather than mailing a dead AP inbox. `invoice.create()` resolves + snapshots only when a payer is found, so the inserted row is byte-identical for the (dominant) self-pay case.

**Reroute (`invoice-email.js`):** when an invoice carries a payer snapshot, the email auto-routes to the payer's AP inbox (`payerRecipient` → role `payer`). Precedence: an explicit operator one-off override still wins; a payer with no usable AP email falls back to the customer billing contact (never strands the invoice). `invoiceRecipientFor` now honors an override `role`. PDF `billBlock` renders **Bill-To = payer** + **Service address = homeowner**, and the meta block shows the PO. Same attach is wired into the `admin-projects` WDO+invoice bundle. Receipts stay customer-routed in Phase 1.

**Assignment + UI:** `/api/admin/payers` CRUD (admin-only); `payerId` accepted on customer `PUT /:id` (account default) and `payerId`/`poNumber` on `PUT /admin/schedule/:id/update-details` (per-job, `cols`-guarded). New `/admin/payers` management page (Finance nav) + a default-payer selector on the Customer 360 Billing tab + a "Bill to (third-party payer)" + PO control on the Edit-appointment modal. Tests: `payer-service.test.js` (resolution precedence, fail-soft) + payer-reroute cases in `invoice-email-recipient.test.js`.

**Phase 2 (not built):** NET terms → accrue to a consolidated monthly statement per payer instead of an instant invoice; PO **hard** enforcement; tech-completion "Billed to … — don't collect on site" banner (land after the CompletionPanel rebuild to avoid double work).

**Codex round 23 hardening (GitHub bot — 1 P2 + 1 P3 on the round-22 head).** (1) **P2 — payer tax exemption lost on invoice EDIT (`invoice.js`).** `create()` forces `taxRate=0` for a tax-exempt payer, but `calculateUpdateFinancials` (the `update()` recalc) re-taxed any commercial invoice from the customer property type alone — so editing a line item on a tax-exempt payer invoice before sending put tax back on the AP total. The recalc now reads the exemption off the invoice's frozen `payer_id` (direct `payers` lookup, degrades to normal tax if the table doesn't exist yet / payer inactive) and skips tax when exempt. (2) **P3 — estimate-accept advertised a suppressed payer pay link (`estimate-public.js`).** Round 21 nulled `invoicePayUrl` for payer invoices but left `invoiceMode`/`invoiceLinkDelivered` set, so `buildAcceptSuccessPayload` still returned `nextStep:'pay_invoice'` and `buildAcceptNotificationPayload` told the customer to "use the invoice pay link" (falling back to `/?tab=billing`) with no usable link. Added a `payerBilled` flag threaded to both builders: the homeowner gets a "sent to your billing contact — nothing due" message and no pay-invoice next-step, while the **admin** copy still correctly says the invoice was sent (so `invoiceMode`/`invoiceLinkDelivered` are intentionally left intact rather than zeroed, which would have falsely told the admin "invoice not sent"). 59 payer-suite tests green.

**Codex round 22 hardening (GitHub bot pass on the clean head — 4 P2s, all payer-subsystem polish).** The local pre-push hook was P0:0/P1:0; the GitHub `@codex` bot then surfaced four P2 suggestions on `3448cbece`, several siblings of earlier fixes. (1) **`previewInvoiceTotals` per-job payer (`invoice.js`)** — the dry-run tax preview resolved the payer from `scheduledServiceId` only, so a `serviceRecordId`-linked WDO/report preview ignored a tax-exempt per-job payer and showed tax the real (exempt) invoice won't bill; now derives `scheduled_service_id` from the service record first (mirror of the round-21 `create()` fix). (2) **`/api/billing/balance` unbounded scan (`billing-v2.js`)** — finding the latest non-payer attempt loaded the customer's entire paid/failed/refunded ledger; now keeps the `.first()` fast path when the customer has no payer invoices and uses bounded paging (50/page, 500 cap) otherwise. (3) **Project send dry-run routing (`admin-projects.js`)** — the `dry_run` confirm-dialog preview reported homeowner self-pay routing even for payer-billed sends; it now resolves the payer (persisted snapshot, or the customer/per-job default for a brand-new preview) and returns `payer_billed`/`report_only` + the payer AP recipient, matching what the real send does. (4) **Override + unattachable payer PDF (`invoice-email.js`)** — an explicit recipient override skipped the payer guard, so a payer invoice whose payer can't attach (legacy/no-snapshot/deactivated) rendered the homeowner as Bill-To to the AP recipient; now synthesizes the same "Third-party payer" placeholder the public PDF routes use before building the attachment (the no-override branch still fails closed). 59 payer-suite tests green.

**Codex round 21 hardening — a P0 estimate-accept pay-token leak + two payer-creation gaps, all rooted in `InvoiceService.create()` now auto-resolving a default payer.** (1) **P0 — public estimate accept returned the payer's pay token (`estimate-public.js`).** The invoice-mode accept path returned `inv.token` as `invoicePayUrl` to the homeowner; with `create()` auto-setting `payer_id` for a customer with a default payer, that handed the homeowner the payer's bearer `/pay/:token` link while the invoice was emailed to the AP. Added one guard after all invoice-id reassignments (covers the billByInvoice, converter, and annual-prepay paths): resolve the final invoice's `payer_id` and null `invoicePayUrl` when payer-billed, which also suppresses the client `pay_invoice` next-step (gated on the URL). (2) **P1 — `serviceRecordId`-only invoices ignored per-job payer overrides (`invoice.js`).** `create()` resolved the payer from `scheduledServiceId` only, but completion-time callers pass `serviceRecordId`; it now derives the visit's `scheduled_service_id` from the service record before resolving, so a job-level Bill-To override on a completed visit bills the right party (the row's own `scheduled_service_id` linkage is unchanged). (3) **P1 — the customer AI minted a payer draft before redacting it (`tools-expanded.js`).** `send_payment_link` excluded *existing* payer invoices but still called `create()` when none existed; for a customer with a default payer that minted a payer-billed draft just to return `payer_billed`. It now resolves the effective payer first and returns the redacted response **without** minting.

**Codex round 20 hardening — draft payer invoices no longer fall back to a stale snapshot AP email (P1).** The round-16 unfrozen branch in `attachToInvoice` only *overwrote* the snapshot AP email when the live active payer had a valid one — so when the live payer was active but its `ap_email` was cleared, the invoice kept the (possibly stale) creation-snapshot AP email and `sendInvoiceEmail` / the recipient preview / project send could deliver to that old address. For unfrozen (draft/scheduled/sending) invoices the live ACTIVE payer now fully controls AP routing: use its current AP email if valid, otherwise **clear** the snapshot AP email (`snap.ap_email = null`) so `payerRecipient()` returns null and delivery fails closed. Identity stays for display. Test: unfrozen-clears-stale-AP-when-live-has-none in `payer-service.test.js`.

**Codex round 19 hardening — the admin invoice recipient preview is now payer-aware (P1).** `getInvoiceDeliveryRecipients` (`/admin/invoices/:id/recipients`) selected only the customer + `notification_prefs`, so for a payer-billed invoice it reported the homeowner's SMS/email. `AdminInvoicesPage` gates Send Invoice / Send Receipt / Record-Payment-receipt off this endpoint, so a payer invoice with an AP email but no homeowner contact was shown as undeliverable (Send disabled), and a homeowner-phone-only account offered receipt-via-SMS — which the server suppresses as `payer_billed`, leaving the AP receipt unsent. Now, when `invoice.payer_id` is set, the endpoint attaches the payer (`PayerService.attachToInvoice`) and returns the payer AP (`payerRecipient`) as the only email recipient with **no** SMS recipient and a `payerBilled: true` flag; an unattachable/AP-less payer reports no recipient so Send stays disabled until the operator adds an AP email — matching the server's fail-closed send behavior.

**Codex round 18 hardening — payer payment failures no longer rescore the homeowner's health (P1).** `handlePaymentIntentFailed` (and the refund/batch paths) rescore the customer via `customerHealth.scoreCustomer(payment.customer_id)`, and `computePaymentScore` (`customer-health.js`) reads the customer's `invoices`/`payments` and penalizes the score for late/failed rows — but payer-billed invoices (and the payments linked to them via `metadata.invoice_id`) are stored under the homeowner's `customer_id`, so an AP payment failure was lowering the *homeowner's* health/risk score and surfacing payer AR as customer delinquency. Fixed at the **scorer** (not just the webhook trigger) so it also covers the nightly batch rescore and any other caller: `computePaymentScore` resolves the customer's payer-billed invoice id set once and excludes payer rows (invoices by `payer_id`; payments by `metadata.invoice_id` → payer invoice) before counting on-time/late/failed, over-fetching to keep a representative self-pay sample. Degrades to no-exclusion if the `payer_id` column doesn't exist yet (migration not run). The webhook rescore call sites are left as-is since the recompute is now correct regardless of what triggered it.

**Codex round 17 hardening — the last payer-balance leak in the customer AI lookup (P1).** `lookup_customer` (`tools.js`) summed every failed/overdue `payments` row for the homeowner `customer_id` into `outstandingBalance` with no payer exclusion — the sibling of the round-14 `getBillingInfo` fix — so an AP payment failure could still surface as the homeowner's balance through the assistant. Extracted the exclusion into shared helpers `payerInvoiceIdSet()` + `isPayerPaymentRow()` (so the two AI lookups can't drift) and applied it to both `lookup_customer` and `getBillingInfo`; matches the `/api/billing` (billing-v2.js) filter. No payer payment row (linked via `metadata.invoice_id` to a `payer_id` invoice) now reaches any customer-facing assistant balance/history.

**Codex round 16 hardening — a P0 in-person collection leak + a fail-closed gap in the round-15 attach change.** (1) **P0 — charge-now REUSE could hand a payer invoice token to tech checkout (`admin-schedule.js`).** The round-7 guard on `POST /:id/invoice` only checks the *current* service/customer payer resolution (`resolveForInvoice`); if the live payer link was cleared/deactivated after an invoice was minted, that resolution reads self-pay and the guard passes. The reuse branch then applied prepaid credit and returned the *existing* invoice's `token` — the AP's bearer pay link — letting the tech collect the AP's bill from the homeowner in person. Now rejects (400, same message as the fresh-mint guard) when `existing.payer_id` is set, before any credit or token is returned. (2) **P1 — unfrozen invoices attached a stale snapshot for a deactivated payer (`payer.js`).** The round-15 change still always assigned the snapshot to `invoice.payer` and only refreshed the AP email when the live payer was active, so a draft/scheduled/sending invoice whose payer was deactivated after minting would still deliver to the stale snapshot AP inbox. `attachToInvoice` now splits cleanly: an **issued** invoice (`sent_at`/frozen status) keeps its immutable snapshot (recovering a live AP only if the snapshot never had one); an **unfrozen** invoice requires a live **active** payer and is left **unattachable** (`invoice.payer` unset → delivery fails closed for operator correction) when the payer is missing/inactive. Tests: unfrozen-deactivated-is-unattachable + issued-keeps-frozen-when-deactivated in `payer-service.test.js` (the prior "does NOT recover from a deactivated payer" case was rewritten — its old null-AP attach is now a fail-closed non-attach; the JSON-string-parse case was made issued so its no-live-query assertion still holds).

**Codex round 15 hardening (post-merge deep pass) — three structural footguns where payer state could still escape its guards (P1×3).** (1) **Dispatch completion returned the payer pay token (`admin-dispatch.js`).** Round 5 stopped opening the in-person payment sheet for payer completions (`invoicePaymentActionRequired`), but the response still returned `invoiceToken` — the AP's bearer pay link (`/api/pay/:token`). A cached/mobile client or the tech holding the response could open it and collect the AP's bill from the service recipient. Now nulled when `invoice.payer_id` is set (mirrors the round-5 `track-public.js` suppression); id/status/total still returned for display. (2) **Resend could overwrite the frozen AP email (`payer.js` + `invoice.js`).** Round 12 froze the delivered AP email on *issued* invoices by reading `invoice.status`, but `sendViaSMSAndEmail` claims a sendable invoice by flipping its status to `'sending'` (`claimInvoiceForSend`) BEFORE `attachToInvoice` runs — so resending an already-sent/viewed payer invoice looked undelivered and replaced the frozen snapshot AP email with the live payer email. `attachToInvoice` now decides "issued" from the persistent `invoices.sent_at` (COALESCE-set on first delivery, survives the claim), falling back to the status set. (3) **Deleting a payer nulled the invoice guard (`migration 20260617000002`).** `invoices.payer_id` was `ON DELETE SET NULL`, but it's the flag every fail-closed path keys off — a payer delete would strand `payer_snapshot` while making the invoice look self-pay, re-exposing the payer's invoice/pay/receipt to the homeowner. Changed to `ON DELETE RESTRICT`: an issued invoice's bill-to is immutable; payers are deactivated (`active=false`), never hard-deleted (no DELETE route exists), so this only blocks a raw delete of a payer that still carries billing history. `customers.payer_id` / `scheduled_services.payer_id` stay `SET NULL` (live reassignable links, no snapshot).

**Codex round 14 hardening (post-`origin/main` merge) — the customer-facing AI assistant was the last surface that could leak a payer invoice to the homeowner (P1×2).** Merging main (which carried the AI assistant's payment tools unchanged) re-exposed sibling paths the earlier rounds closed on the server routes. (1) **`send_payment_link` (`tools-expanded.js`)** auto-selected the most recent unpaid invoice with no `payer_id` exclusion and returned the pay URL — so a homeowner asking the assistant for a payment link could be handed the *payer's* pay link (and round 10's `sendViaSMSAndEmail` branch would silently bill the AP off a homeowner chat). The auto-select now `whereNull('payer_id')`, and an explicit payer `invoice_id` returns a redacted `{ payer_billed: true }` (no send, no pay URL) — the payer is billed only through the admin/dispatch payer-send path. (2) **`check_payment_status` (`tools-expanded.js`)** selected payer invoices and returned `cardBrand`/`cardLastFour`/status — the payer's card details to the homeowner; now excludes `payer_id` on auto-select and redacts an explicit payer id to `{ payer_billed: true }`. (3) **`getBillingInfo` (`tools.js`)** — the AI mirror of the `/api/billing` balance/history that rounds 6–8 hardened — read raw `payments` by `customer_id`, which includes payer payment rows (they sit under the homeowner but join to a `payer_id` invoice via `metadata.invoice_id`); it now drops those rows from `recentPayments`/`outstandingBalance` using the same invoice-id-set filter as `billing-v2.js`. (4) **`POST /admin/invoices/:id/send` `saveBillingRecipient` (`admin-invoices.js`)** persisted a one-off AP override into the **homeowner's** billing prefs without checking `payer_id`, which would reroute that homeowner's own future self-pay invoices to the third party; the save is now gated on `!invoice.payer_id` (payer AP delivery persistence is handled by `payer.freezeApEmail`). The same `origin/main` merge reconciled the App.jsx/AdminLayoutV2 nav with main's Documents→Contracts consolidation (#1872), keeping the new Payers/Finance entry alongside Contracts.

**Codex round 13 hardening (same PR) — three "looks delivered / stays unsent" bookkeeping gaps (P2).** (1) **Project combined-send surfaces a missing payer AP** — when a payer invoice has no usable AP email, `payerBilled` is false; the route now records an explicit `channels.payer_email` failure AND folds the payer leg into the project's `delivered`/`deliveryStatus` (a payer project isn't "delivered" until BOTH the homeowner report and the payer invoice go out). Previously the homeowner-report success marked the project delivered while the invoice was silently restored to draft and the AP never got it. (2) **Schedule LIST returns `payerId`/`poNumber`** — `/admin/schedule/list` didn't select them, but the Edit-appointment modal opened from the list echoes them on save, so a normal save posted blank `payerId`/`poNumber` and silently cleared an existing per-job Bill-To/PO (and tripped the admin-only actual-change 403 for techs). Added both to the list select + payload (matching the detail endpoint). (3) **Auto receipt queue stamps `receipt_sent_at` for payer invoices** — a payer-billed receipt skips the homeowner SMS path (where `sendReceipt` normally stamps `receipt_sent_at`), so the auto queue left the invoice in `needs_receipt` forever and a batch/manual resend duplicated the AP receipt; the queue now stamps it when the payer AP email delivers.

**Codex round 12 hardening (same PR) — the AP email is frozen ON DELIVERY, not creation (+ fail-closed everywhere).** The clarifying model from this round, consistent with the round-3 intent ("an *issued* invoice keeps its Bill-To"): the snapshot freezes the bill-to **identity** (name/address) at creation, but the **AP email** (delivery address) is only frozen once the invoice is issued/delivered. (1) **`attachToInvoice` prefers the live active payer AP email for UNDELIVERED invoices (P2)** — `AP_FROZEN_INVOICE_STATUSES` (sent/viewed/overdue/paid/prepaid/processing/terminal) gates it: a draft/scheduled/sending invoice tracks the live payer's current AP email so an operator's correction takes effect on a resend; an issued invoice uses the frozen snapshot. This fixes the stale-AP-on-retry case for **both** `sendInvoiceEmail` and the project combined-send (both call `attachToInvoice`), not just the flagged path. (2) **Shared `PayerService.freezeApEmail` (P2)** — the round-11 persist logic moved into `payer.js` and is now also called by the project payer-send (`admin-projects`) after `channels.payer_email` succeeds, so a recovered/corrected AP email is frozen regardless of which path delivered it. (3) **Dispatch already-delivered set includes `overdue` (P2)** — an overdue pre-minted invoice reused on a delayed completion no longer re-sends a duplicate AP email. (4) **Fail-closed placeholder extended to receipt JSON + both PDF routes (P2)** — `receipt-v2` JSON, the `/pay/:token/invoice.pdf`, and `/receipt/:token/pdf` now render a "Third-party payer" placeholder (not the homeowner) when `payer_id` is set but the payer can't attach, matching the round-11 pay-page fix. Tests: issued-vs-undelivered AP resolution in `payer-service.test.js`.

**Codex round 11 hardening (same PR) — persistence/dedup/fail-closed follow-ons (+ a jsonb-mutation bug).** (1) **Persist the delivered AP email, not just one-off overrides (P2)** — `persistPayerApIfNeeded` now freezes the AP email the invoice was actually delivered to (live-recovered, operator one-off, or first send of a legacy invoice) onto `payer_snapshot`, no-op once the snapshot already carries it; previously a *recovered* AP email (round 5) was delivered but never persisted, so a later payer edit/deactivation stranded the receipt/pay-page bill-to. **Bug found doing this:** `attachToInvoice`'s recovery mutated the snapshot object **in place** (`parseSnapshot` returns the jsonb-as-object by reference), so the persist check saw the email "already there" and skipped — `attachToInvoice` now clones the snapshot before filling the recovered email. (2) **Gate dispatch completion payer send to unsent invoices (P2)** — `invoiceCreated` is also true when a completion REUSES an existing unpaid invoice (pre-minted `sent`/`viewed`, or `invoiceAlreadySent`); the payer send now skips already-delivered statuses so it can't duplicate the AP billing email (fresh completion invoices are `draft`). (3) **Recipient-versioned project payer key (P2)** — the round-10 stable key dedup'd forever even after the AP email changed, so a corrected-and-retried `/send-with-invoice` returned the old blocked/bounced result; the key now includes a sha1 of the AP email — dedupes a repeat to the same inbox, re-delivers to a corrected one. (4) **Pay page fails closed for unattachable payers (P2)** — `pay-v2` serialized `payer:null` when `payer_id` was set but the payer couldn't attach (legacy, no snapshot, inactive/deleted payer), and the React page rendered that as self-pay with the homeowner as bill-to; it now serializes a "Third-party payer" placeholder so the page stays non-self-pay (save-card suppressed, billing email blank). Tests: live-recovered-AP snapshot-persist case in `invoice-email-recipient.test.js`.

**Codex round 10 hardening (same PR) — fail-closed keying + two SMS-only/retry stragglers.** (1) **Reroute keyed on `payer_id`, not the attached object (P1, hole in round 4).** `sendInvoiceEmail` / `sendReceiptEmail` keyed the payer reroute/fail-closed branch off `invoice.payer` (the attached object). A payer-billed invoice whose payer can't be attached (no snapshot + live payer inactive/missing) left `invoice.payer` unset, so the branch was skipped and the invoice/pay-link (or receipt with the payer's card last4) fell through to the homeowner — exactly what every prior round forbade. Both now key off `invoice.payer_id` and **fail closed** when no payer recipient resolves. (2) **AI `send_payment_link` tool (P2)** — `tools-expanded.js` called `sendViaSMS` directly, which short-circuits to `payer_billed` for payer invoices (no AP email, no finalize); it now routes payer invoices through `sendViaSMSAndEmail` (shape-agnostic `sent` from `sent||ok`), mirroring the round-8 batch fix. (3) **Duplicate payer invoice on report retry (P2)** — the `admin-projects` combined-send finalizes the invoice off the payer AP delivery even when the homeowner report leg fails, so a `/send-with-invoice` retry re-billed the AP a duplicate invoice/pay-link (the idempotency key carried a per-call timestamp). The payer copy now uses a **stable** `project.report_with_invoice:{project}:{invoice}:payer` key — dedupes after the first success, still retryable after a genuine failure. Tests: payer-can't-attach fail-closed cases (invoice + receipt) in `invoice-email-recipient.test.js`.

**Codex round 9 hardening (same PR) — symmetric ACH guard, a hole in my round-7 fix, and the one-off-AP-recipient end-to-end gap.** (1) **ACH success state reset (P1, symmetric to round 6)** — `payment_intent.succeeded`'s `us_bank_account` branch reset the homeowner's `ach_status='active'`/`ach_failure_count=0` off the payer payment's `customer_id`; now guarded so a payer/AP bank clearing can't reactivate a homeowner's suspended ACH. (2) **Blocked payer-completion send marked delivered (P1, hole in round 7)** — `sendInvoiceEmail` returned `{ok:true}` even when SendGrid resolved `sent:false` (recipient suppressed/unsubscribed), so the round-7 dispatch finalization (which keys solely off `.ok` because the homeowner SMS is suppressed) could mark a never-delivered payer invoice as sent. `sendInvoiceEmail` now returns `{ok:false, blocked}` on `sent===false`; the dispatch gate is unchanged (fixed at the source, benefits every caller). (3) **Payment plans rejected for payer invoices (P1)** — `POST /admin/invoices/:id/payment-plan` 400s for payer-billed invoices before inserting a homeowner-scoped plan / pausing follow-ups (round 6 only suppressed the confirmation email; a payer-facing plan flow is Phase 2). (4) **Payer name PII in logs (P1)** — `admin-payers` create log drops the `display_name`, logging only the payer id. (5) **One-off AP recipient now end-to-end (P2)** — when a payer with no AP email is invoiced via an explicit operator one-off recipient, `sendInvoiceEmail` freezes that AP email onto `invoices.payer_snapshot.ap_email` on a successful send, so the (async) receipt and the pay page route to the same AP contact the invoice was billed to instead of resolving no recipient / prefilling the homeowner. (6) **History limit vs payer filter (P2, finally robust)** — `/api/billing` now pages through history (via a new `getPaymentHistory(customerId, limit, offset)`) excluding payer rows until `limit` customer-visible payments are filled or the table is exhausted (bounded ~10 pages), replacing the `limit*3+10` heuristic — no metadata-cast over the whole table. (7) **Pay-page billing email (P2)** — `PayPageV2` no longer prefills the homeowner's email into Stripe billing details for a payer invoice; it passes the payer email or leaves it blank for the AP to enter. Tests: blocked-send `ok:false` + one-off-AP snapshot-persist cases in `invoice-email-recipient.test.js`.

**Codex round 8 hardening (same PR) — a self-inflicted regression + two completeness gaps.** (1) **`/api/billing` history `ReferenceError` (regression from round 7).** The round-7 over-fetch rewrite dropped the `const { limit } = req.query` destructuring, so `parseInt(limit)` threw on every authenticated billing-history request (no route-level test covers this handler, and `node --check` can't catch a runtime `ReferenceError`). Restored as `parseInt(req.query.limit)`. (2) **Upcoming/next-charge balance leak** — round 6/7 filtered payer-linked `failed` rows from `/api/billing/balance` but left the `upcoming` sum + `nextPayment` reading every `status='upcoming'` row, so a payer-linked upcoming autopay row still showed in the homeowner's `upcomingCharges`/`nextCharge`. Both now apply the same `isPayerPayment` exclusion. (3) **Batch immediate-send stranded payer invoices** — `POST /admin/invoices` with `sendImmediately` called only `sendViaSMS`, which short-circuits to `payer_billed` and never finalizes; payer-billed batch rows now route through `sendViaSMSAndEmail` (payer AP email + finalize) while self-pay keeps the SMS-only immediate send. Note: the round-7 regression shipped because the billing-v2 route handlers have no test coverage (the repo's route tests exercise `_private` helpers, not HTTP handlers); the fixes here were verified by `node --check` + identifier audit rather than a new bespoke harness.

**Codex round 7 hardening (same PR) — stranded payer AR + the last collection/dunning siblings.** (1) **Stranded payer AR on dispatch completion (the one real bug, self-inflicted in round 4).** Suppressing the homeowner completion-SMS pay link for payer invoices left the auto-created invoice delivered to nobody — the homeowner channel can't finalize it and there's no payer send in that handler. The dispatch completion path now routes a payer-billed auto-invoice to the payer AP inbox (`sendInvoiceEmail`) and finalizes on success (`markDeliverySent({ email: true })`); a payer with no usable AP email leaves it unfinalized for operator correction (never mails the homeowner). (2) **Charge-now pre-completion mint** — `POST /admin/schedule/:id/invoice` (the tech-checkout in-person collection mint) now resolves the payer and 400s for payer-billed visits, so the sibling of the round-6 terminal-handoff guard can't collect the AP's invoice from the homeowner either. (3) **Balance-reminder balance math** — `getCustomerBalance` now excludes payer-linked `failed`/`upcoming` payment rows before computing `totalBalance`/`daysOverdue` (round 6 only filtered the oldest-invoice pay link; an AP ACH failure row still inflated the homeowner's balance and could trigger an early reminder). (4) **Bill-to routing is audited** — a `payer_id` change on a customer is now in `sensitiveFields`, so redirecting a customer's invoices to a different AP account writes a `customer.update_sensitive` audit entry. (5) **History limit vs payer filter (P3)** — `/api/billing` over-fetches before excluding payer rows so a homeowner whose newest payments are AP payments still gets up to `limit` visible self-pay rows. Tests: balance-reminder mock updated for the new payer-ids lookup.

**Codex round 6 hardening (same PR) — the adjacent paths behind each round-5 fix.** Round 5 fixed the primary surface of each leak; round 6 closes the sibling path that shares the same data. (1) **Charge endpoints reject payer invoices server-side** — `StripeService.chargeInvoiceWithSavedCard` throws and `POST /api/stripe/terminal/handoff` 400s for a payer-billed invoice, so a stale client or direct admin/tech call can't charge the homeowner's saved card / mint an in-person handoff for the AP's bill (the round-5 dispatch flag only hid the UI). (2) **ACH failure webhook** — `handleAchFailure` early-returns for a payer-billed invoice (looked up by the PI), so an AP bank failure never mutates the homeowner's `ach_status`/card-default or texts them retry/suspension notices. (3) **ACH processing webhook** — the `payment_intent.processing` handler returns before its direct `ach_payment_processing` SMS for payer invoices (the `sendAchProcessing` email already self-guards, but the SMS is sent inline). (4) **Refund / payment-plan / retry lifecycle emails** — `sendRefundIssued`, `sendPaymentPlanConfirmed`, and `sendPaymentRetryNotice` resolve the linked invoice and return `payer_billed` for payer invoices, so refunding the AP's payment or putting a payer invoice on a plan no longer emails the homeowner. (5) **Legacy balance-reminder cron** — `BalanceReminder.getCustomerBalance` + `latePaymentCheck` exclude `payer_id` invoices when picking the "oldest unpaid invoice" pay link (the round-5 fix only covered `LatePaymentService`; the balance-reminders job is a second overdue path). (6) **Customer balance — failed payments** — `/api/billing/balance` now excludes payer-linked `failed` payment rows from `currentBalance` and the `lastPaymentFailed` banner (round 5 only filtered the unpaid-invoice sum; an AP ACH/card failure row sits under the homeowner's `customer_id`). (7) **Manual offline payments** — `POST /admin/invoices/:id/record-payment` stamps `metadata.invoice_id` on the `payments` row for payer-billed invoices so the customer-facing history/balance filters catch them; self-pay rows stay unlinked to preserve the existing receipt-total fallback. Tests: refund + payment-plan `payer_billed` skips in `payment-lifecycle-email.test.js`.

**Codex round 5 hardening (same PR) — close the last homeowner-leak channels + the snapshot strand.** Round 4's "never bill/chase the homeowner" principle, applied to every remaining surface a payer invoice could leak through. (1) **Project combined-send billing copy** — the self-pay billing-contact fallback (`else if (channels.email?.ok)`) is now gated on `!isPayerInvoice`, so a payer invoice with no usable AP email is simply not delivered (operator fixes the AP email) instead of mailing the homeowner the third-party invoice + pay link. (2) **Dispatch mobile collection** — `invoicePaymentActionRequired` now gates on `!invoice.payer_id`, so a payer-billed completion never opens the in-person payment sheet (techs must not collect AP's invoice from the service recipient). (3) **Customer tracker** — `track-public.js` suppresses `invoiceToken` for payer-billed invoices, so a homeowner with the public track link can't open the payer's `/pay/:token` page. (4) **Stripe lifecycle emails** — `sendPaymentFailed` + `sendAchProcessing` (payment-lifecycle-email.js) early-return `payer_billed` for payer invoices; those notices resolve recipients off `invoice.customer_id` (homeowner) with the pay link, so the homeowner is no longer told the payer's card failed / ACH is processing. (5) **Legacy late-payment-checker** — its overdue query now excludes `payer_id` invoices (the new follow-up short-circuit only covers the new sequence; the legacy cron selected unhandled overdue invoices and texted/emailed the homeowner). (6) **Customer billing balance** (`/api/billing/balance`) excludes payer invoices from `currentBalance`, so the homeowner doesn't see the payer's unpaid amount as their own. (7) **Customer payment history** (`/api/billing`) drops rows whose `metadata.invoice_id` joins to a payer-billed invoice, so the homeowner never sees the payer's card brand/last4/Stripe PI id. (8) **Snapshot AP-email strand** — `attachToInvoice` recovers the live AP email from the still-active payer row when the frozen snapshot has none (invoice minted before ops filled it in), without disturbing the frozen name/address identity; otherwise round-4's no-homeowner-fallback would strand that invoice forever even after the AP email is corrected. (9) **Recurring payer/PO-only edits** — `PUT /admin/schedule/:id/update-details` now propagates a parent payer/PO change to pending child visits independently of the date/cadence rewrite gate, so editing only the Bill-To on a series reaches future visits. Tests: snapshot AP-email recovery (+inactive-payer guard) in `payer-service.test.js`; lifecycle-email `payer_billed` skips in `payment-lifecycle-email.test.js`.

**Codex round 4 hardening (same PR) — never bill or chase the homeowner for a payer invoice.** The round-3 principle (a misconfigured payer must not leak onto the homeowner) is now applied to the remaining channels. (1) **Invoice email no longer falls back to the homeowner** — a payer-billed invoice with no usable AP email (and no explicit operator one-off override) now FAILS (`sendInvoiceEmail` returns `ok:false`) instead of routing the PDF + pay link to the customer billing contact; the operator adds the payer AP email (or a one-off recipient) and resends. This covers the normal/batch/scheduled send paths that share `invoiceRecipientFor`. (2) **Receipt email is payer-only** — a payer receipt goes to the payer AP inbox or NOT at all (no homeowner fallback that would expose the payer's payment-method last4); a missing AP email returns the standard "No receipt recipient email" skip. (3) **Receipt SMS suppression is non-retryable** — `actionableSmsFailure` now treats `payer_billed` like `already-sent`/`no-phone`, so the receipt delivery queue stops retrying/failing a job whose homeowner SMS was intentionally suppressed. (4) **Dispatch completion SMS** drops the pay link for payer-billed jobs (`allowCompletionInvoiceLink` gates on `!invoice.payer_id`) — the homeowner still gets the report-only completion text, AR routes to the payer. (5) **Invoice follow-ups never arm for payer invoices** — `scheduleForInvoice` short-circuits on `invoice.payer_id` (centralized, so `markDeliverySent`/project-send and every other caller are covered), so the dunning sequence can't chase the homeowner with the payer's pay link. Phase 1 has no payer dunning sequence (Phase 2). Tests: invoice-email no-fallback (+override-still-sends) and receipt payer-only routing in `invoice-email-recipient.test.js`; `payer_billed` non-retry in `receipt-delivery-queue.test.js`.

**Codex round 3 hardening (same PR).** (1) **Bill-to is now snapshotted, not just FK'd** — `invoices.payer_snapshot` (jsonb) freezes the payer name/company/AP-email/address at creation; `attachToInvoice` prefers the snapshot (no live query, no active dependency), so an issued invoice/receipt keeps its original Bill-To even if the payer is later renamed/edited/deactivated. Legacy pre-snapshot invoices fall back to the live row (active-guarded). (2) **Homeowner gets a report-ONLY email** for payer invoices (`sendProjectReportReady` with the FDACS PDF + report link, no invoice PDF / pay link); the invoice + pay link go to the payer. (3) **Project suppression keys off `invoice.payer_id`** (`isPayerInvoice`), not AP-email availability — a misconfigured payer (active, no `ap_email`) still never bills the homeowner, and the invoice simply isn't finalized (can't deliver to the payer). (4) **Receipt JSON + ReceiptPage** serialize/show the payer Bill-To (matching the PDF). (5) **Receipt SMS suppressed** for payer invoices (`sendReceipt` returns `payer_billed`) — never texts the homeowner a receipt that would expose the payer's card last4. (6) **`previewInvoiceTotals`** resolves the payer and applies `tax_exempt`, so the WDO confirmation total matches the created invoice. (7) **PO field shows for the EFFECTIVE payer** (`form.payerId || customer.payerId`) so a default-payer job can capture a PO. (8) **Pay page** no longer posts `/consent` for payer payments (clears the stale `?saveCard=1` parent state → no spurious `consent_failed` banner).

**Codex round 2 hardening (same PR) — reroute now covers every money channel.** (1) **Save-card** guard extended to `updateInvoicePaymentIntentMethod` + `finalizeInvoicePayment` (not just create) — an AP user toggling "save card" after the Element loads still can't attach to the homeowner. (2) **Receipt email** reroutes to the payer AP inbox (symmetric with the invoice email). (3) **Pay-link SMS** to the homeowner is suppressed for payer invoices — guarded at the source in `sendViaSMS` (restores the send-claim) and short-circuited in `sendViaSMSAndEmail`; the project combined-send SMS drops the pay-link line (keeps the report link). (4) **Recurring children** inherit the (freshly-updated) parent's `payer_id`/`po_number` on both new-child spawn and existing-child rewrite, so a series doesn't silently revert to self-pay. (5) **Pay page** (`GET /api/pay/:token`) attaches + serializes the payer; `PayPageV2` shows Bill-To = payer / Service address = homeowner + PO, hides the save-card consent, and prefills Stripe billing_details with the payer (not the homeowner). (6) **Project combined-send**: payer AP delivery is now INDEPENDENT of the customer/report email and the invoice is finalized on `payer_email` success (`invoiceDelivered`), so a payer invoice can't be marked sent without the AP inbox receiving it, nor stranded when the homeowner has no email. (7) **Tech 403 regression** fixed — the schedule edit modal echoes payer/PO on every save, so the admin-only gate now fires only on an ACTUAL change vs the stored values. (8) **Per-job dropdown** label is truthful: blank = "Use account default — <name>" when the customer has a default payer, else "Customer pays (self)". Known Phase-2 gap: no explicit one-off self-pay override when a default payer exists (would need a sentinel/flag).

**Codex round 1 hardening (same PR):** (1) **Tax-exempt is wired** (owner-ratified) — a tax-exempt payer forces `taxRate=0` in `invoice.create()`, zeroing tax even on commercial jobs; cert stored for records. `previewInvoiceTotals()` preview not yet exemption-aware (cosmetic; the saved invoice is authoritative) — Phase 2. (2) **Saved-payment opt-in suppressed for payer invoices** — `createInvoicePaymentIntent` forces `saveCard=false` when `invoice.payer_id` is set, so the AP contact's card can never attach to the homeowner's Stripe customer. (3) **Per-job lookup scoped by customer** — `resolveForInvoice` constrains the `scheduled_services` lookup by `customer_id` so a stale/mismatched `scheduledServiceId` can't snapshot another customer's payer. (4) **Inactive payer never attaches** — `attachToInvoice` mirrors `resolveForInvoice`'s `active !== false` guard (a payer deactivated after mint falls back to self-pay on send). (5) **Token/printed PDFs attach the payer** — `/api/pay/:token/invoice.pdf` and `/api/receipt/:token/pdf` attach before rendering so downloaded docs show the same Bill-To. (6) **Project WDO+invoice billing copy routes to the payer AP inbox** (fallback to customer billing contact). (7) **Per-job payer/PO edits are admin-only** on `PUT /admin/schedule/:id/update-details` (route is requireTechOrAdmin; payer routing must not be tech-settable). (8) **PO is advisory** (owner-chosen) — relabeled; the appointment editor shows a non-blocking "usually requires a PO" reminder. (9) Partial payer updates accept snake_case `display_name` (UI rename bug). (10) `resolveForInvoice` now returns `{ payerId, poNumber, taxExempt }`.

## 2026-06-17 — Invoice prepaid status + customer account credit (claude/invoice-prepaid-marking-tibmi3)

**Decision (owner spec 2026-06-17):** an invoice can be marked **prepaid** by drawing down a customer's account-credit balance — the quarterly-prepay flow — and that credit is attributed to the customer via a ledger. Four owner decisions drove the build: (1) credit applies **manually** (operator click), never auto-deducted, to avoid racing Stripe autopay; (2) `prepaid` is a **real new invoice status**, distinct from Stripe-collected `paid`; (3) **no recurring prepay discount** — only an optional waive of the WaveGuard initial/setup fee, recorded as a flag (mirrors the annual-prepay `setupFeeWaived` display flag; does NOT recompute line-item totals); (4) operator surfaces are the **Invoice detail page** and **Customer 360**, no Intelligence Bar tool.

**Account credit is now real.** `customers.account_credits` (added but never read/written since 20260401000085) becomes a cached running balance. New append-only `customer_credit_ledger` (migration 20260617120000) records every signed movement (`delta`, `balance_after`, `source`, optional `invoice_id`). `services/customer-credit.js` is the single writer: `postCreditMovement` locks the customer row, recomputes, refuses to go negative, and writes cache + ledger in one transaction (optionally folded into a caller's trx). Sources: `manual` / `adjustment` / `invoice_application` / `invoice_prepaid` / `referral`.

**Endpoints.** `GET|POST /admin/customers/:id/credits` (balance + history; issue/adjust — admin-only, audited as `customer.credit.adjust`). `GET /admin/invoices/:id/credit-context` (balance + amount due for the modal). `POST /admin/invoices/:id/apply-credit` (admin-only): locks the invoice, draws down credit up to the amount due, increments `invoices.credit_applied`, and — when fully covered — flips status to `prepaid` (+`prepaid_at`/`prepaid_by`), stops the follow-up sequence, and writes a `payments` ledger row so revenue dashboards count the coverage. Partial application reduces the balance due and leaves the invoice collectible.

**`prepaid` is terminal/uncollectible.** Added to `INVOICE_UNCOLLECTIBLE_STATUSES` (invoice-helpers.js) — so `assertInvoiceCollectible` blocks re-payment on the public pay page (pay-v2 already routes every collect path through it) and the invoice stats exclude it from outstanding/overdue. Treated like `paid` where "money's in": receipt PDF + receipt send (receipt-v2, invoice.sendReceipt), send-invoice guard, Customer 360 `amount_paid`, list status color/badge, and the new `Prepaid` list filter (`directStatuses`). Receipts for credit-prepaid invoices behave exactly like manual-cash-payment receipts (the `payments` row carries no `invoice_id`, so `loadPaymentForInvoice` returns null and the generator falls back to invoice totals — same as the existing manual path).

**Revenue recognition (called out for owner ratification):** account credit is a holding bucket (issuing credit writes NO `payments` row); revenue is recognized when credit is **applied** to an invoice (the apply-credit `payments` row, amount = applied). This keeps prepaid money as deferred until tied to a serviced invoice and avoids double-counting. The invoice-level `total_collected`/`paid` stats still count only `status='paid'`, so prepaid sits in its own bucket rather than the invoice-based collected figure.

**Referral credit deliberately NOT wired (deferred).** Referral rewards already accrue to a separate promoter wallet (`promoters.available_balance_cents` etc.) with its own `pending`→`earned`→`credited` lifecycle; auto-posting them into `account_credits` would double-credit live payouts. `customer_credit_ledger.source` reserves the `referral` value and a nullable `referral_id` so a later reconciliation PR needs no migration.

**UI.** Invoice detail (Tier 2, `D` palette): new `ApplyCreditModal` + "Apply credit" action — shows available credit vs amount due, optional waive-setup-fee, partial/full preview, "Apply & mark prepaid". Customer 360 (Tier 1 V2, components/ui): new `AccountCreditPanelV2` on the Billing tab — balance, ledger history, admin-only Issue/Deduct credit form.

**Codex review follow-up (same PR).** Hardened the new status against its downstream blast radius: (1) **partial credit application removed** — apply-credit now requires credit to cover the invoice in full (a partial application would leave the invoice collectible while the Stripe/Terminal pay paths still price off `invoice.total`, over-collecting); to prepay part of a bill, lower the invoice first. (2) The prepaid transition now **cancels any open PaymentIntent** first (refusing if money is in flight, mirroring the cancelled-service triage) so a stale session can't charge the card after the credit is consumed. (3) It **stamps `paid_at`** alongside `prepaid_at` so AR/outstanding dashboards (`paid_at IS NULL`) and annual-prepay term activation (keyed on `status='paid' || paid_at`) treat it as closed; `syncTermForInvoicePayment` is now invoked on the transition. (4) `assertInvoiceVoidable` rejects `prepaid` (voiding would strand the consumed credit — reverse the credit instead); the generic invoice edit path is edit-locked when `credit_applied > 0` (same rationale as deposit-credit invoices). (5) Receipts wired for prepaid on the remaining guards (`/send-receipt` route, `/batch/send-receipts`, `sendReceiptEmail`); the credit `payments` row carries `metadata.invoice_id` so receipt rendering + the cancelled-service money guard see it. (6) PayPage redirects `prepaid` to the receipt; Customer 360 `balanceOwed` excludes `prepaid`; the `setup_fee_waived` column now feeds the customer-facing `setupFeeWaived` callout. **Still deferred:** there is no credit-reversal/undo flow for a prepaid invoice (void is blocked) — a mistaken prepaid needs manual correction; a proper reverse-and-restore-credit action is a follow-up.

**Codex re-review follow-up (revenue recognition — owner decision).** Codex flagged that booking a paid `payments` row on every credit application would report goodwill/courtesy credit as collected/taxable income. Owner decision: **recognize cash when it is RECEIVED, not when applied.** Issuing credit now takes a funding kind — `prepayment` (money received: cash/check/Zelle/card) books a paid `payments` row at issuance; `goodwill` and `adjustment` are non-cash and book nothing. `apply-credit` no longer inserts a `payments` row at all (prevents double-counting cash and taxing courtesy credit). Customer 360's Issue-credit form gained the Funding (prepayment vs goodwill) + Method selectors and an inline note of the revenue effect. Also closed the remaining collection guards so a prepaid invoice can't be double-collected: record-payment's race guard uses `INVOICE_UNCOLLECTIBLE_STATUSES`, and the Terminal handoff mint + PI-create re-verify reject `prepaid`; `needs_receipt` list + the customer ReceiptPage now include prepaid.

**Codex round-4 follow-up (prepaid receipts + reversal — owner decisions).** The proactive "prepaid invoices get receipts" wiring kept surfacing payment-received copy across every channel (SendGrid + SMTP email, SMS, receipt PDF, public ReceiptPage), which is misleading for goodwill/account-credit coverage. Owner decision: **do not send payment receipts for prepaid invoices.** Reverted prepaid out of the receipt paths (`sendReceiptEmail`, `/send-receipt` + `/batch/send-receipts`, `InvoiceService.sendReceipt`, `receipt-v2` PDF + state, `needs_receipt` list, admin Download-PDF/Send-receipt buttons, client ReceiptPage). Instead, the customer pay link renders a friendly **"You're all set — nothing due · covered by your account credit"** state in `PayPageV2` (no payment receipt, no charge UI). Second owner decision: **added a reversal path** — `POST /admin/invoices/:id/reverse-prepaid` (admin-only, + a "Reverse prepaid" button on prepaid rows) restores the consumed credit to the customer (a `+adjustment` ledger movement) and reopens the invoice to `sent`; the issuance cash row is intentionally left (the money is held as credit again). Also excluded `prepaid` from the AI assistant's unpaid-invoice payment-link selector (`tools-expanded.js`) so it can't try to bill a covered invoice.

## 2026-06-18 — Lawn Care Re-Service (claude/lawn-care-reservice-waves-di4frf)

**Decision:** add a **Lawn Care Re-Service** to the Service Library, mirroring the existing **Pest Control Re-Service** (`pest_re_service`) one-for-one for the lawn-care line — a free callback visit between regular service intervals for active recurring lawn-care customers experiencing breakthrough weed / disease / insect pressure. Single additive migration `20260618000001_lawn_re_service.js`; no runtime code change.

**Why migration-only:** the re-service concept is already fully generic. The `is_callback` flag and the dispatch callback routing / service-record / document callback copy all key off the `"Re-Service"` (or `"callback"`) name, so naming the row **"Lawn Care Re-Service"** picks up all of that automatically. Admins select it from the new-appointment modal exactly like the pest re-service: it ships `customer_visible: false` / `booking_enabled: false` (internal, not self-bookable) but `is_active: true`, and `GET /admin/services` filters on active only, so it surfaces in the admin service lookup.

**Service row** (`lawn_re_service`): category `lawn_care`, `billing_type: 'one_time'`, `pricing_type: 'variable'` / `base_price: null` (no charge for active WaveGuard / recurring lawn-care customers), `is_taxable: true` / `tax_service_key: 'lawn_care'`, `requires_license: true` / `license_category: 'L&O'`, `icon: '🔁'`, `sort_order: 14` (after the lawn family). Tax key + license category follow the rest of the lawn catalog (`pest_re_service` used `pest_control` / `GHP`).

**Completion profile:** seeded directly in the post-cutover shape — `completion_mode: 'service_report'`, `project_type: 'one_time_lawn_treatment'`, `portal_visibility: 'token_only'`, `portal_attach_policy: 'recurring_customer'` — matching the rest of the lawn family (`lawn_aeration` / `lawn_fungicide` / `lawn_insect_control` / `lawn_inspection`) after the Phase-1 cutover (`20260611000012`). `PROJECT_TYPE_BY_SERVICE_KEY` already routes `/^lawn_/` to `one_time_lawn_treatment`, so no separate cutover migration is needed — lawn re-service completions render through the typed lawn CompletionPanel + Service Report V1, the same end state `pest_re_service` reached.

**Codex review follow-up (owner: "fix both pest + lawn"):** Codex flagged two real gaps in the *shared* re-service design (pre-existing — they affected `pest_re_service` identically; this PR did not introduce them). Owner directed fixing both lines, so the fix is service-key-aware rather than lawn-only. (1) **Auto-callback flag** — the new-appointment modal never sends `isCallback`, and downstream callback reporting (`service_records.is_callback`) + document PDF copy (`documents.js` `is_callback`) read the persisted column, not the service name. New `server/services/re-service.js` (`isReService` / `RE_SERVICE_SERVICE_KEYS = {pest_re_service, lawn_re_service}`); the scheduler (`admin-schedule.js` POST `/`) now derives `is_callback` from the catalog row, so both re-services persist the flag and flow into callback metrics + the "no additional charge" PDF copy. (2) **Free callback could bill monthly dues** — a re-service for a WaveGuard customer zeroes `estimated_price` at scheduling, and completion fell back to `monthly_rate` (`admin-dispatch.js` invoice path, and the one-time completion billing guard `projectCompletionInvoiceAmount` in `project-completion.js`, which would otherwise 409-block or invoice a month's dues). Both now skip the `monthly_rate` fallback when `is_callback` is set — an explicit positive price still bills if the operator set one. Regression coverage added in `tests/project-completion.test.js`.

## 2026-06-19 — Restore the Generate-AI-report button + corner dictation mic in CompletionPanel (claude/pest-control-ai-bart-voice-nef2bf)

**Decision (owner directive 2026-06-19):** partially reverse the Phase-2 CompletionPanel simplification (#1875, b274498). The owner uses the **manual "Generate AI report"** button daily — the tech enters brief structured notes, taps the button, and AI drafts customer-facing visit copy into the Technician Notes box for them to review/edit before completing. #1875 removed that button on the premise that report copy would be generated server-side at completion, but the tech-facing draft-and-edit workflow is still wanted, so the button is restored. The Phase-3 "auto-derive at completion" path is unaffected — the two are complementary (this just gives the tech an editable draft in-box).

**Restored verbatim from b274498's parent:** the module-level `generateAiReport(payload)` fetch helper (`POST /api/admin/schedule/generate-report` — the endpoint was never removed, `admin-schedule.js:4535`), the `buildAiReportPayload()` method (classifies inputs by provenance so the prompt won't promote a recommendation/concern into a confirmed finding), the `generating` state, and the `!quickComplete`-gated Generate button in **both** CompletionPanel render variants (mobile `M` palette + desktop `D` palette). Behavior is 1:1 with the pre-#1875 implementation; button label gains a ✨ prefix.

**Dictation mic relocated to the notes-box corner (owner: "little microphone ... in the bottom right").** The `useSpeechDictation` voice-to-text (added in #1875) is unchanged; only its control moved. The wide "🎙 Dictate notes" pill below the textarea is replaced by a small circular mic button absolutely positioned in the **bottom-right corner of the Technician Notes textarea** (both variants). The textarea reserves right-side padding (`paddingRight` 52 mobile / 50 desktop when `dictation.supported`) so typed text never runs under the mic; idle shows 🎙, listening shows a red ■ stop glyph. Falls back gracefully (no mic) on browsers without the Web Speech API.

## 2026-06-19 — Commercial proposal PDF + multi-building line items (claude/siesta-key-pest-estimate-o18m9e)

**Decision (owner ask):** for commercial leads (the Siesta Key HOA case — two towers + 50 lake houses), turn an estimate into a formal, sendable **line-item proposal PDF** built from a **multi-building** model, and **attach the PDF to the estimate delivery email** (SMS keeps texting the estimate link — carriers can't attach files).

**Multi-building model — JSONB, no migration.** The proposal lives in `estimates.estimate_data.proposal` (the table already carries a `category: COMMERCIAL` enum + JSONB `estimate_data`). Shape: `{ enabled, title, preparedFor, propertyAddress, taxRate, taxLabel, terms, buildings: [{ name, note, lineItems: [{ description, quantity, unitPrice, frequency, taxable }] }] }`. `frequency ∈ monthly|bimonthly|quarterly|annual|one_time`. `server/services/estimate-proposal.js` is the single source of truth: `normalizeProposal` (reads the authored proposal, else **synthesizes** a single-building fallback from engine line items / stored totals so any estimate can still produce a PDF) + `computeProposalTotals` (annualizes by cadence → annual recurring + monthly equivalent + one-time + first-year total).

**Tax is not re-implemented here.** Taxability is CPA-signed and owned by the tax module; this feature only sums the per-line `taxable` flags the operator sets and applies the proposal's `taxRate`. With no rate set (the residential-HOA default — common-area pest non-taxable, lawn never taxable in FL) tax is $0 and every line renders non-taxable. The PDF marks taxable lines with `*` and notes the rule.

**PDF.** `server/services/pdf/estimate-pdf.js` (pdfkit), reusing invoice-pdf.js chrome 1:1 — navy masthead with logo + FDACS license, branded footer, zinc rules. Renders per-building sections with a line-item table (description / cadence / qty / rate / amount), per-building subtotal, a totals block (monthly equiv · annual recurring · one-time · tax · **first-year total**), and a Terms & assurances block (FDACS license, COI-on-request, IPM + callback guarantee). Multi-page paginator (`ensureSpace`) re-prints a slim continuation header + table header across pages (verified at 14 buildings / 7 pages).

**Routes (admin-estimates.js, admin-auth):** `GET /:id/proposal` (normalized proposal + totals), `PUT /:id/proposal` (author/replace — recomputes the three authoritative total columns from the line items, since the operator-entered items ARE the commercial quote, and stamps `category=COMMERCIAL`), `GET /:id/proposal.pdf` (inline branded PDF — same generator as the email attachment, so download and emailed copy are byte-identical). **Email attachment:** `sendEstimateNow` builds the attachment **only when `proposal.enabled`** (an authored proposal) — synthesized fallbacks are NOT attached, so ordinary residential estimate emails are unchanged; PDF failure is non-fatal (link email still sends). Threaded through `sendEstimateEmail` → SendGrid `attachments` (base64) with a nodemailer conversion for the SMTP fallback path. Not an Intelligence Bar tool, so no write-gate registration.

**UI (Tier 1, components/ui).** New self-contained `client/src/components/estimates/CommercialProposalModal.jsx` opened from a **"Commercial proposal"** row action in `EstimatesPageV2` (desktop pipeline). Add/remove buildings + line items, per-line cadence + taxable toggle, tax-rate field, live totals (client mirror of `computeProposalTotals`), **Save proposal** (PUT) + **Download PDF** (adminFetch → blob → new tab; admin auth is a bearer token, so a plain anchor won't carry it). Kept as an isolated component + 4 small edits to the 3.8k-line page (import, state, menu item, modal render) to minimize blast radius.

## 2026-06-19 — Third-party payer Phase 2 — statement close + NET-terms delivery (feat/payer-statements-close-deliver)

**Decision:** build the close + deliver layer on top of the merged accrual core (#1929), completing the NET/consolidated-statement path Phase 1 deferred (see the 2026-06-17 entry — Phase 1 wired only `due_on_receipt`; a payer on `net15`/`net30` accrues each month's billed visits onto one OPEN `payer_statements` row). Phase 2-here turns that open row into a sent, AP-processable document: **finalize (freeze) → render PDF → email the payer's AP inbox**, operator-driven from the admin payer routes, shipped dark behind `GATE_PAYER_STATEMENTS`.

**Finalize (`finalizeStatement`, payer-statements.js):** freezes totals + the bill-to snapshot + the NET due date and flips `open → finalized` inside a transaction. Concurrency mirrors accrual exactly: it takes the **same per-(payer, period) advisory lock** as `getOrCreateOpenStatement` FIRST, then row-locks the statement `FOR UPDATE` before freezing — so a late visit either attaches before the freeze, or finds the statement non-open and opens the next period (never lands after close, never races the total). Idempotent: a non-open statement is returned unchanged. The due date is statement-dated NET in ET (`etDateString(addETDays(date, termDays))`, `net15`→15 / `net30`→30, default 30); `overdue` stays **derived** from `due_date`, never stored (carried from the P1 design). The frozen `payer_snapshot` is refreshed from the live payer at close (mirrors `invoices.payer_snapshot`) but a payer-read failure never blocks the close — it falls back to the statement's existing snapshot.

**Ledger + PDF.** `loadStatementLines` returns the attached non-void invoices as a chronological visit ledger (homeowner name + service address per line). `server/services/pdf/payer-statement-pdf.js` (pdfkit) renders one consolidated NET-terms statement — a line per visit + rolled-up totals — from the **FROZEN snapshot, never the live payer**, so a reprint always matches what was billed (reuses invoice-pdf.js chrome 1:1; multi-page paginator).

**Delivery (`payer-statement-email.js`) carries the P1 invariant end-to-end: a statement bills the PAYER, never the resident.** The AP recipient resolves **only** from the frozen snapshot, with the live payer's AP email as a *recover-missing* fallback — there is no homeowner fallback. **No AP email ⇒ the send fails loudly** (`no_ap_email`) rather than mis-billing a homeowner. Send path: SendGrid template `payer.statement.sent` (seeded in `20260620000002` — a `transactional_required` billing template so it's never marketing-suppressed; the SMTP path remains a dev/safety fallback caught via `template not found`), PDF attached, then stamps `finalized → sent` + `sent_at` atomically (`WHERE status='finalized'` so a viewed/paid statement is never downgraded and a resend never re-stamps). Only billed-deliverable statuses are sendable (`finalized`/`sent`/`viewed`) — `open` returns `statement_not_finalized`, `void`/`paid`/anything else `statement_not_sendable`, so a voided statement can never reach AP rendered as "Due". `dryRun` builds the PDF + resolves the recipient WITHOUT sending or stamping (for the dry-run-first rollout + admin preview).

**Routes (admin-payers.js, admin-auth + requireAdmin).** `GET /:id/statements` (recent), `GET /:id/statements/:sid` (statement + lines), `POST …/close` (txn-wrapped finalize; `{ send, dryRun }` chains the AP send so "close & send" is one click), `POST …/send` ((re)send a closed statement; 409 while still open). Every statement route is **ownership-scoped** (`loadOwnedStatement` 404s if the statement's `payer_id` ≠ the addressed payer, so one payer's URL can't reach another's). Read paths are ungated (return `[]` until the gate flips); the mutating close/send paths are gated on `payerStatements`. The send runs **outside** the close transaction (never hold a DB txn across an email send).

**Codex pre-push follow-up (2 rounds, all P1 — no P0).** Round 1: (1) AP email no longer logged (PII — log statement/payer ids + counts); (2) close-and-send no longer reports a failed AP delivery as success (accurate log + 422 mirroring `/send`, frozen statement still returned since re-close is idempotent); (3) overdue computed in **ET not UTC** — `new Date('YYYY-MM-DD')` compared UTC midnight and could flag a statement overdue the prior evening in America/New_York; new `isStatementOverdue` compares the due calendar day vs today in ET (`dateOnlyString` + `etDateString`). Round 2: (4) **seeded the `payer.statement.sent` template** (above) so a prod send isn't a guaranteed `email_unavailable` dead-end once the gate flips; (5) **status allowlist** so a `void`/`paid` statement can't be emailed as due. Round 3 (1 P0 + 1 P1): (6) **P0 — finalize lock key now matches accrual.** `period_start` comes back from the DATE column as a JS Date; interpolating it raw produced `Fri May 01 2026 …` while accrual locks on `${pid}|YYYY-MM-DD`, so the two never shared the advisory lock and a late invoice could attach after the freeze. Normalized via `dateOnlyString` (regression test asserts the Date case). (7) **P1 — first-delivery idempotency key** (`payer_statement_sent:<id>`) so a double-click / retry / concurrent close-and-send can't email AP twice (`sendTemplate` dedupes only on `idempotencyKey`); an explicit resend stays keyless and intentional. Round 4 (1 P1): (8) the `/close` chained send is now **first-delivery-only** — it sends only when the frozen row is genuinely pre-send (`finalized`, no `sent_at`); an idempotent re-close that returns an already-`sent`/`viewed` statement skips the send (`{ skipped: 'already_delivered' }`, not a 422) so a double-click can't mail AP a duplicate after the first-delivery key has lapsed. Resends still go through `/send`. Round 5 (1 P1): (9) the PDF "Issued" row rendered `finalized_at` (a TIMESTAMP) via `dateOnly` (UTC date-only), so a 10pm-ET close showed the next day — switched to `dateTime`/`formatDisplayDate` (ET calendar date); the DATE columns (period/due/service dates) correctly stay on `dateOnly`. Round 6 (1 P1): (10) a **blocked first delivery was unretryable** — `sendTemplate` writes a terminal `blocked`/`bounced` row under the stable first-delivery key (those are in `DEDUPE_STATUSES`), so reusing it deduped forever. Added a `forceResend` flag for the retry. **Round 7 reconciles rounds 6+bot into a force path** (the GitHub bot flagged that a blanket-keyless `/send` would double-send a *first* delivery on a double-click — the exact inverse of round 6): a normal send (`/close` chained or plain `/send`) keeps the stable first-delivery key (dedupes double-clicks); `POST /send { force: true }` is the ONLY keyless first-delivery path, used to retry a known blocked/suppressed attempt that the terminal key would otherwise dedupe forever. Already-sent re-delivery stays keyless. **GitHub bot P2 follow-ups (2 rounds):** `force` no longer goes keyless at all. `forcedRetryKey` walks past each generation whose attempt terminally blocked (base → `:r1` → `:r2` …, checking `email_messages`) to the first non-blocked generation's key. The result is **fresh** for a new generation (so a genuinely blocked statement can be retried) yet **stable** within it — so a double-click or two concurrent forced requests dedupe on `:rN` (the `email_messages` unique key resolves the race) instead of each inserting a keyless row and double-sending. A stray force with no prior block returns the base key unchanged; fails safe to the base key (never keyless) on a lookup error. **`forceResend` is routed through `forcedRetryKey` for ANY status, not just `finalized`** — so a statement SendGrid accepted (stamped `sent`) then bounced async via webhook is still generation-scoped on a force retry rather than falling to the keyless already-sent branch. Force with nothing to retry resolves to the base key and dedupes against the delivered row (no blind resend). **Close-chain concurrency:** the `/close` chained send passes `firstDelivery: true`, which PINS the base key regardless of the row's status at send time — so two concurrent close-and-sends (one stamps `sent` between the other's freshness check and its re-read) dedupe on the base key instead of the late one going keyless. **PDF property column** now renders homeowner name AND service address (a consolidated statement to a property manager / HOA spans many homes, so AP needs the serviced location, not just the name). **Dedupe-loser handling:** when two first-delivery requests race, `sendTemplate` raises `EMAIL_SEND_IN_PROGRESS` for the loser while the winner's row is still `queued`; the loser now returns `{ ok: true, deduped: true }` (and does NOT stamp `sent` — the winner does) instead of a false 422 AP-delivery failure.

**Deferred to a later Phase 2 slice:** month-end auto-close cron (today close is operator-triggered), payer-portal statement view + online pay, PO enforcement, payer deposit roll-forward/refund, and the tech-completion "Billed to … don't collect on site" banner (lands after the CompletionPanel rebuild). 25 tests green (`payer-statements.test.js`, `payer-statement-email.test.js`, `payer-statement-overdue.test.js`).

## 2026-06-21 — Third-party payer Phase 2 — P3 (pay + settle) (feat/payer-statements-pay-settle)

**Decision:** add statement payment + settlement on top of the merged accrual (#1929) + close/deliver (#1941) lanes — AP settles a finalized statement online (self-serve Stripe on the payer's customer) AND/OR offline (check/ACH/wire reconciled by admin), and settlement CASCADES to every accrued child invoice. Gated behind `GATE_PAYER_STATEMENTS`. Owner decisions (2026-06-19): offer both online + offline; card-save OPTIONAL with NO silent auto-charge on due_date.

**Status state machine (`payer-statement-settle.js`).** `open → finalized → sent → viewed → processing → paid` (or `void`). PAYABLE = `finalized`/`sent`/`viewed` (frozen + not-in-flight) — a PaymentIntent may be created only from these. **`processing` is entered ONLY on a CONFIRMED money-in-flight webhook** (`payment_intent.processing` for ACH / `succeeded` for card), never on PI creation — an unconfirmed PI stays replaceable, so merely opening or abandoning the pay page can't lock the statement. Once `processing`, a second pay confirm AND admin reconcile are both refused. `overdue` stays derived from `due_date`, never stored. `settleStatementPaid` cascades (statement `paid` → child invoices `paid` with `paid_at = statement.paid_at`, a settlement marker not N charges → ONE payer-scoped `payments` row), idempotent on already-paid; the offline reconcile passes a PAYABLE-only allowed-status set so it can't settle a statement whose online payment is already in flight (double collection).

**Payments ledger.** Migration `20260621000001` adds `payments.statement_id` (FK→payer_statements) + `payments.payer_id` (FK→payers) and makes `customer_id` NULLABLE — a statement settlement writes ONE row with `customer_id = NULL`, `payer_id`/`statement_id` set, `amount` = the CHARGED total (surcharged for a card; base/surcharge split on the existing `*_cents` columns). Only **customer-keyed** readers exclude payer-scoped rows (per the design wording): the per-customer revenue breakdown in `dashboard-tools` adds `whereNull('payer_id')` so a `customer_id = NULL` settlement row isn't shown as a bogus "no customer" bucket; per-customer queries elsewhere are already `customer_id = X` filtered (NULL excluded). **Business-wide cash/revenue totals INCLUDE the payer settlement row** — it's real cash, counted once (the child invoices get no separate payment rows, so there's no double-count). See round 8/9 below — an earlier over-application of the exclusion to global totals was reverted.

**Self-serve pay (`pay-statement.js` at `/api/pay/statement`, mounted BEFORE `/api/pay` so its two-segment paths aren't shadowed by the invoice `/:token`).** The statement's own `token` resolves it; `GET` stamps `viewed` (sent→viewed) and returns the visit ledger + bill-to; `setup` → `quote` → `finalize` mirror the invoice surcharge two-step but charge **`payer.stripe_customer_id`** (new `ensureStripePayerCustomer`, kept separate from the homeowner flow). Surcharge runs the same `computeChargeAmount(total, methodType, { funding })` quote→finalize as invoice card pay (statements are NOT deposits → surcharge applies normally; rate derived, never hardcoded); ACH/offline carry no surcharge. `setup` reuses a replaceable `requires_payment_method` PI / cancels other unconfirmed states / refuses real in-flight money — and never moves the statement to `processing`.

**Webhook (`stripe-webhook.js`).** A PI carrying `metadata.waves_statement_id` routes to `handleStatementPaymentIntentEvent` at the top of each PI handler and returns — legacy `invoice_id` intents are unchanged. Idempotent, keyed on the active PI: `processing` → `processing`; `succeeded` → settle + cascade (surcharge cents derived from the PI); `payment_failed`/`canceled` → revert to the derived prior payable status (collectible again). NOT feature-gated — a confirmed money event must settle regardless of the flag.

**Admin reconcile (`admin-payers.js` `POST …/statements/:id/reconcile`).** Offline settle (check/ACH/wire) + cascade; refuses while `processing`/`paid`; **cancels any unconfirmed online PI first** (`cancelStatementPaymentIntentIfUnconfirmed`, 409 if money is truly in flight) so the AP can't also pay online after the operator records the check. 36 payer tests green. **Deferred to P4:** AR/aging view + statement-level dunning (`payer_statement_followups`).

**Codex pre-push round 1 (4 P0 + 1 P1).** (P0) (1) the new public `/api/pay/statement/:token` surface is now in the AGENTS public-by-token allowlist with a contract, plus a 64-hex token-format gate + per-IP rate limit on the route. (2) **Surcharge-bypass quarantine** — setup mints a base-amount, client-confirmable PI, so a credit-card payer could skip `/quote`+`/finalize` and confirm at base; the webhook now runs the SAME `shouldQuarantineUnfinalizedCardPayment` guard as invoices before settling and quarantines+alerts a card that succeeded without surcharge finalization (no base-only settle). (3) **Active-PI binding** — the succeeded webhook now locks the statement and settles only when the succeeded PI is the statement's CURRENT `stripe_payment_intent_id`; a stale/replaced PI that collected money is an orphan/over-collection → alert for manual refund, never settle. (4) **Reconcile fails closed** — if an existing statement PI can't be retrieved/verified, `cancelStatementPaymentIntentIfUnconfirmed` now throws 409 (was: proceed), so an offline reconcile can't double-collect against a still-confirmable client secret. (P1) the dashboard `paidRevenueTotal`/`paidRevenueDaily` ledger sums also got the `whereNull('payer_id')` payer-row exclusion.

**Codex pre-push round 2 (5 P0).** (1) **Stale surcharge metadata on PI reuse** — a reused `requires_payment_method` PI reset to base kept its old `surcharge_policy_version` (Stripe metadata merges), which the webhook reads as "finalized" → would settle a later base-only card confirm without surcharge; the base reset now explicitly clears `surcharge_policy_version`/`surcharge_rate_bps`/`card_funding` (empty string deletes the keys). (2) **Reconcile ↔ setup race** — a concurrent `/setup` could mint a new confirmable PI between the reconcile's cancel and settle; cancel + settle now run UNDER ONE `forUpdate` lock (which `/setup` also takes), so no new PI can appear in the window. (3) **Wallet surcharge exemption** — the reused invoice quarantine helper exempts wallets; a credit Apple/Google Pay confirmed at base would settle undercharged. Added an `exemptWallets` option; the statement caller passes `false` (full card-family surcharge). (4) **Durable alerting** — statement quarantine/orphan alerts hit `customer_health_alerts` (customer_id NOT NULL) and silently failed; they now write a durable `stripe_orphan_charges` row (tolerates null customer; the operator's manual-refund queue), throwing so the webhook retries until persisted. (5) **Public payload PII** — the by-token route returned `loadStatementLines` wholesale (includes `customer_name`); it now whitelists serviced address + visit fields, no homeowner name.

**Codex pre-push round 3 (3 P0).** (1) **Settlement wrote a non-existent column** — the `payments` insert set `payment_method`, but `payments` has only `payment_method_id` (FK), so EVERY settlement insert would have thrown and rolled back the paid cascade after Stripe may have collected; the method now rides `metadata` (and `payer_statements.payment_method`). (2) **Reconcile fail-open when Stripe down** — `cancelStatementPaymentIntentIfUnconfirmed` returned a no-op for an unconfigured Stripe BEFORE checking for an existing PI; it now loads the statement first and throws 409 if a PI exists but Stripe can't verify it (can't double-collect a still-live client secret). (3) **Statement chargebacks left the statement paid** — the invoice-keyed dispute handler no-ops on a statement payment (keyed by `statement_id`, no `invoice_id`), hiding clawed-back money; added `reverseStatementCascadeForDispute` (created/lost → statement back to owed + children reopened) and `restoreStatementCascadeForDispute` (won → re-settle unless re-collected), keyed on `payment.statement_id`.

**Codex pre-push round 4 (1 P0 + 2 P1).** (P0) the dispute reversal now also clears `payer_statements.stripe_payment_intent_id`/`stripe_charge_id` — otherwise `/setup` + reconcile see the old succeeded PI as active and 409, so the reopened AR could never be re-collected (the disputed `payments` row keeps the PI for audit). (P1) the settled method is derived from the actual attached PaymentMethod (`paymentDetailsFromIntent`) not the PI's allowed-types list — a base-amount debit/prepaid card was being recorded as ACH (the PI allows both). (P1) the remaining IB revenue readers got the `whereNull('payer_id')` exclusion too (`dashboard-tools` MTD/last-month/per-customer/monthly-trend, `tax-tools` two YTD sums) — a final sweep confirms every paid-payment aggregate now excludes payer-scoped rows.

**Codex pre-push round 5 (2 P0).** (1) **PI replacement now fails closed on a cancel error** — `createStatementPaymentIntent`'s reuse branch logged a failed cancel and minted a replacement anyway; if the old PI had raced into processing/succeeded its client secret could still collect → double charge. It now throws 409 unless Stripe confirms the old PI is canceled. (2) **Dispute reversal is now PI-scoped** — `reverseStatementCascadeForDispute`/`restoreStatementCascadeForDispute` take the disputed payment's PI and no-op unless the statement is still settled by THAT PI, so a late `dispute.closed(lost)` for PI A can't undo a replacement settlement (PI B / offline) the AP made after `dispute.created` reopened it.

**Codex pre-push round 6 (2 P0).** The statement succeeded webhook was reworked to trust NOTHING from PI metadata. (1) **Active-PI binding is now a non-null exact match** — it settles only when `stmt.stripe_payment_intent_id === piId` (a null/different stored PI ⇒ stale/orphan/replaced ⇒ record a review item, never settle). (2) **Surcharge is recomputed from the ACTUAL confirmed funding** — `computeChargeAmount(statement.total, methodType, { funding })` from `paymentDetailsFromIntent`, and the charged amount must match (±1¢) or it quarantines. This replaces the metadata-trusting `shouldQuarantineUnfinalizedCardPayment` for statements (a failed `/finalize` could leave a stale `surcharge_policy_version` on a reusable PI, letting the same client secret confirm a different tender — credit at debit base, or debit with a stale credit surcharge). Settlement now writes the recomputed cents, bound to the real tender. (The invoice path keeps the original helper unchanged.)

**Codex pre-push round 7 (3 P0 + 1 P1).** (1) **Self-deadlock fix** — the webhook settle passed `database: trx` inside the settlement payload, but `settleStatementPaid` takes it as the THIRD arg, so it ran on the global `db` and blocked forever on the outer txn's `FOR UPDATE`; now `settleStatementPaid(id, settlement, { database: trx })`. (2) **Active-PI check moved BEFORE the idempotent-paid shortcut** — a stale/replacement PI succeeding after the statement was paid another way now records a `stripe_orphan_charges` review item instead of a silent skip. (3) **Dispute-won restore guards replacements** — it no-ops when the statement is `processing` or carries a different active PI (AP started a replacement after `dispute.created`), instead of overwriting it. (P1) reconcile validates the amount against the LOCKED `total` inside the txn (a close/reroll between the pre-lock read and the lock could change it).

**Codex pre-push round 8 (1 P0).** Fail closed on UNVERIFIED card funding — `paymentDetailsFromIntent` swallows a Stripe charge/PM lookup failure and leaves `funding` null, so a card PI (created at base) confirmed without `/finalize` would recompute against `funding: null` (no surcharge) and settle undercharged. The succeeded handler now records a manual-review `stripe_orphan_charges` row and does NOT settle when a card-family PI has unverifiable funding (ACH is unaffected — it carries no surcharge).
