## 2026-07-07 — Admin shell scroll polish: containment, motion-safe smooth jumps, thin scrollbars, route reset (claude/waves-admin-scrolling-y1y4yf)

**Context.** Owner report: scrolling in the admin portal feels clunky. The V2 shell locks the window (`.admin-shell-v2` is `overflow: hidden`) and scrolls everything inside `.admin-main`, with nested overflow panes on most pages (thread lists, dropdowns, detail panels). Four concrete sources of clunk: (1) wheel/swipe at the end of a nested pane chained into the page behind it (and iOS pull-to-refresh tugged on the PWA shell); (2) navigating between admin routes preserved the previous page's scroll offset — pages opened mid-scroll, and React Router's window-based restoration can never reach a nested scroller; (3) programmatic jumps teleported, and two "back to top" calls targeted `window`, which never scrolls in this shell (silent no-ops — Communications SMS-log reply); (4) chunky UA scrollbars on every pane plus horizontal layout shift between short and long pages. Researched against current best practice (MDN `overscroll-behavior`/`scrollbar-gutter`, Chrome scrollbar-styling guidance, Smashing on `prefers-reduced-motion`): the fix is native CSS scroll properties, NOT a JS smooth-scroll/lerp library — wheel/trackpad speed is never hijacked.

**Change (all admin-scoped, customer/tech surfaces untouched).**
- `index.css` (new `.admin-shell-v2` block, alongside the existing admin-scoped Roboto block): `overscroll-behavior: contain` on `.admin-main`, the sidebar, and every Tailwind overflow pane (`[class*="overflow-y-auto"]` / `[class*="overflow-auto"]`, `-x` variants for the horizontal strips); `scroll-behavior: smooth` on `.admin-main` guarded by `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference)`; `scrollbar-gutter: stable` + `scroll-padding-top` (12px desktop, 52px-bar + safe-area + 12px mobile, so `scrollIntoView` targets clear the fixed top bar) on `.admin-main`; thin stone scrollbars (`scrollbar-width: thin`, `scrollbar-color: var(--border-strong) transparent`, plus `::-webkit-scrollbar` fallback at 10px with a padded 8px-radius thumb). Scrollbar rules use `:where()` so they cascade at zero specificity — the existing `.horizontal-scroll`/`.tab-pill-scroll` hiding rules and inline styles still win.
- `AdminLayoutV2.jsx`: `mainRef` on `.admin-main` + effect that snaps it to the top on `location.pathname` change with `behavior: "instant"` (animating across a route change is disorienting; query-param-only changes intentionally don't reset so in-page tab/selection params keep their position).
- `CommunicationsPageV2.jsx`: SMS-log reply's inert `window.scrollTo` now targets `.admin-main` (smooth).
- `DashboardPageV2.jsx`: the mobile tab-switch snap passes explicit `behavior: "instant"` so the shell's new smooth default doesn't animate a content swap.

**Verification.** Chromium (Playwright) against the Vite dev server, computed-style + behavior checks on `.admin-main`: `scroll-behavior: smooth`, `overscroll-behavior: contain`, `scrollbar-gutter: stable`, `scroll-padding-top` 12px desktop / 64px at 390px, `scrollbar-width: thin` with `--border-strong` thumb; sidebar contain+thin. Behavioral: bare `scrollTo({top: 800})` animates (mid-flight sample between endpoints), explicit-instant snaps same-frame, and a scrolled container (600px) resets to 0 immediately on sidebar navigation to `/admin/customers`. Screenshots at 1440 + 390 show no shell regression (no backend in-session, so pages rendered their error/empty states). `npm run build` clean incl. brand check. No DB in-session.

## 2026-07-07 — Learn tab feeds: newsletter card thumbnails + Venice→Palmetto local news sources (claude/suncoast-news-sources-xxbtvs)

**Context.** Owner report (portal screenshots): the Learn tab's "Local Suncoast News" card sits on "0 items" and every Waves Newsletter card renders the icon placeholder. Two separate causes. `/api/feed/local` pulled a single source — MySuncoast (WWSB ABC7) local RSS — whose general-news stream (crime/politics/human-interest) rarely survives the strict `RELEVANT_KEYWORDS`/`EXCLUDE_KEYWORDS` filter, so the card is empty outside storm/red-tide news cycles. `/api/feed/newsletter` hardcoded `image: null` (`newsletter-feed.js`) even though every sent body embeds images (generated hero on the S3 CDN, event photos), so the client's existing `post.image` rendering never fired.

**Change (server-only; no client edits — `ContentCard` already renders `post.image` when present).**
- `server/routes/feed.js`: `/local` now fans out to a `LOCAL_NEWS_SOURCES` table — MySuncoast (unchanged) + Sarasota Herald-Tribune (Gannett/FeedBlitz feed), Bradenton Herald (McClatchy rssfeed-widget feed, covers Bradenton/Palmetto), Venice Gondolier (BLOX search RSS) — fetched in parallel, merged, keyword-filtered across the set, interleaved newest-first, capped at 5 (was 3 from one source). Each item carries its outlet as `sourceName`. A dead/moved feed URL logs `[feed] Upstream <key> ...` and contributes zero items — never breaks the endpoint. Publisher domains + image CDNs (gannett-cdn.com, townnews.com bloximages, yoursun.com) added to `ALLOWED_LINK_HOSTS`; upstream fetches now carry a 10s timeout so one hanging publisher can't stall the fan-out.
- `server/services/newsletter-feed.js`: card image = first NON-GIF `<img>` in `html_body` (the `.gif` skip drops the Waves divider and Giphy reaction memes in one rule, including Beehiiv-proxied giphy uploads in imported issues); hero wins when present, event photos back-fill hero-less issues, all-GIF/image-less bodies stay `image: null`. http(s)-only with `url(...)`-breakout characters rejected, mirroring `feed.js` `safeImage` hygiene (the client renders this in a CSS background). Applies to both consumers: portal Learn tab and the public landing past-issues grid.

**Verification.** Jest green: new `feed-local-sources.test.js` (parallel fan-out, per-outlet tagging, cross-source keyword filter, newest-first interleave, 500ing source degrades to zero items, feed-native image vs og:image fallback vs null) and `newsletter-feed-card-image.test.js` (hero wins; divider/giphy GIFs never surface; event-photo fallback; javascript:/relative/breakout srcs rejected; `&amp;` decoded); `feed-blog-og-image.test.js` extended with empty-channel fixtures for the new sources. **Caveat:** the three new feed URLs follow each publisher's platform conventions but could NOT be verified live from the session sandbox (network egress blocks publisher domains). Post-deploy: check Railway logs for `[feed] Upstream heraldtribune|bradenton_herald|venice_gondolier` warnings and swap the URL in `LOCAL_NEWS_SOURCES` if one stays quiet. Observer Media Group (yourobserver.com) deliberately omitted — no discoverable RSS endpoint.

## 2026-07-07 — Local news card: bank matched stories so it always looks full (claude/suncoast-news-sources-xxbtvs, follow-up 2)

**Context.** Owner follow-up to the same-day local-news entries: "keep the older posts in there, so it always looks full." Even with five sources, /api/feed/local served only what currently sat in the publishers' live feeds — each feed carries ~25 recent items, so once a matched story rotated out, the card drained back toward "0 items" between relevant news cycles.

**Change.** New `local_news_items` table (migration `20260707000030`, hasTable-guarded, symmetric down): link (unique, dedupe key), title, description, image, source_name, pub_date timestamptz, created_at. New `server/services/local-news-store.js` (`newLinks` / `insertItems` / `latestItems`, prune to newest 60). The route now banks every story that passes the relevance filter and serves the newest 5 ever seen; og:image is resolved once at ingest and only for genuinely new links (no more per-request page fetches for repeat items). DB unreachable / table missing degrades to the pre-bank behavior (serve the current fetch directly) — never a 500. `pubDate` in the response is now a normalized UTC string rather than the raw feed string (client already parses via `new Date()`).

**Verification.** Feed suites green, including new assertions: a pre-banked story absent from every upstream feed still renders (with its stored image, no page fetch); a second request spends zero og:image fetches and returns a stable list; store-throwing mock proves the degrade path. Migration + store dry-run against a REAL throwaway Postgres 16 in-session (not just mocks): up×2 idempotent, down/up symmetric, 65 inserts prune to 60, conflict-ignore dedupe, newest-first reads, timestamptz round-trips as Date. Not run against a prod-schema mirror (sandbox has no dev-branch DATABASE_URL) — the table is new and self-contained, no existing-schema assumptions. Post-merge: confirm the Railway deploy ran migration 20260707000030 before expecting banked items.

## 2026-07-07 — Billing Preferences delivery-channel dropdowns (claude/waves-portal-dropdown-0uo971)

**Context.** Owner request (screenshot of the portal Billing tab): the two Billing Preferences toggles — "Billing reminder texts" and "Payment confirmation texts" — need the same Text / Email / Both delivery dropdown the appointment reminders got in the 2026-06-22 channel work (migration 20260622000011).

**Change.**
- Migration `20260707000030_billing_notification_channels.js`: `billing_reminder_channel` + `payment_confirmation_channel` on `notification_prefs` (varchar(10), default 'sms' so existing customers see no behavior change). Unlike the appointment channels these are per-row, NOT primary-profile account-level — billing sends target the charged customer row, and the toggles + `billing_email` they sit beside are already per-row (documented in the migration header and the `CHANNEL_DB_COLUMNS` comment in `routes/notifications.js`).
- `routes/notifications.js`: `billingReminderChannel` / `paymentConfirmationChannel` flow through the payload, update mapping, Joi schema, and account.updated change-log labels ("Billing Reminder — Delivery", "Payment Confirmation — Delivery").
- Messaging pipeline: new optional `channelColumn` policy field (`billing` → `billing_reminder_channel`; `payment_receipt` → `payment_confirmation_channel`). The consent validator suppresses the SMS leg with a new `CHANNEL_EMAIL_ONLY` code when the stored channel is 'email' — scoped to `input.channel === 'sms'` so email sends through the wrapper are never blocked by an email-preferring customer. Semantics: Text = today's behavior; Both = texts continue (the billing email lanes — receipt-delivery-queue emails, late-payment/statement emails — already deliver independently); Email = these texts are suppressed and the email lanes carry the notice. Deliberately NOT gated: purpose `payment_link` dunning texts (balance/late-payment pay-link reminders) — those were never gated by the `billing_reminder` toggle either, since a customer can't opt out of being asked to pay; and the `autopay` purpose row is untouched.
- Bug fix riding along: the `payment_receipt` policy row pointed at a `payment_receipt` prefs column that has never existed on `notification_prefs`, so the "Payment confirmation texts" toggle was stored but never enforced at send time. It now points at the real `payment_confirmation_sms` column (defaults true → default-on customers unaffected; only explicit opt-outs stop getting receipt texts, which is what the toggle promised).
- Portal UI (`PortalPage.jsx` BillingTab): Text/Email/Both select on each row, same styling + gating as the Schedule tab appointment selects — Email/Both only offered with an email on file (billing recipient email or account email), select disabled while its toggle is off, saved via Save Billing Preferences (an email-only choice is normalized back to Text on save if the last email was removed).

**Verification.** jest: new `billing-notification-channels.test.js` (consent gate incl. sms-channel scoping, toggle enforcement, route mapping, per-row channel placement) + messaging/notification suites green. Playwright (Chromium against the Vite dev client with a stubbed API): dropdowns render at 1440 and 390 with stored values, grey out when the toggle is off, and the save PUT carries both keys. `check:portal-brand` clean, `vite build` clean. No DB in-session — the migration was not executed against a live database (hasTable/hasColumn-guarded, additive, default 'sms').
